(** general associativity for binary operations on types *)

Section BinaryOperations.

  Context {X:UU} (unel:X) (op:binop X).

  (* we use an extra induction step in each of the following definitions so
     we don't end up with superfluous unel factors *)

  Definition iterop_list : list X → X :=
    foldr1 op unel.

  Definition isAssociative_list := ∏ (x:list (list X)), iterop_list (Lists.flatten x) = iterop_list_list x.

  Definition isAssociative_fun :=
    ∏ n (m:stn n → nat) (x : ∏ i (j:stn (m i)), X), iterop_fun (StandardFiniteSets.flatten' x) = iterop_fun_fun x.

  Definition isAssociative_seq :=
    ∏ (x : Sequence (Sequence X)), iterop_seq (FLists.flatten x) = iterop_seq_seq x.

  Local Open Scope stn.

  Definition isCommutative_fun :=
    ∏ n (x:⟦n⟧ → X) (f:⟦n⟧≃⟦n⟧), iterop_fun (x ∘ f) = iterop_fun x.

append_vec x y ∘ dni lastelement = x

    
X: UU
unel: X
op: binop X
lunax: islunit op unel
m: nat
x: ⟦ m ⟧ → X
y: X
i: ⟦ m ⟧
(append_vec x y ∘ dni lastelement) i = x i

    
X: UU
unel: X
op: binop X
lunax: islunit op unel
m: nat
x: ⟦ m ⟧ → X
y: X
i: ⟦ m ⟧
append_vec x y (dni lastelement i) = x i

    
X: UU
unel: X
op: binop X
lunax: islunit op unel
m: nat
x: ⟦ m ⟧ → X
y: X
i: ⟦ m ⟧
x i = x i

    reflexivity.
  Defined.

End BinaryOperations.

(** general associativity for monoids *)

Local Open Scope multmonoid.

Section Monoids.

  Context {M:monoid}.

  Let oo := @op M.

  Let uu := unel M.

  Definition iterop_fun_mon {n} (x:stn n->M) : M := iterop_fun uu oo x.

  Definition iterop_list_mon : list M → M := iterop_list uu oo.

  Definition iterop_seq_mon : Sequence M → M := iterop_seq uu oo.

  Definition iterop_seq_seq_mon : Sequence (Sequence M) → M := iterop_seq_seq uu oo.

  Definition iterop_list_list_mon : list (list M) → M := iterop_list_list uu oo.

  (* some rewriting rules *)

Section Monoids2.

  Context (M:monoid).

  Let op := @op M.

  Let unel := unel M.

  Definition isAssociative_list_mon := isAssociative_list unel op.

  Definition isAssociative_fun_mon := isAssociative_fun unel op.

  Definition isAssociative_seq_mon := isAssociative_seq unel op.

  Definition isCommutative_fun_mon := isCommutative_fun unel op.

End Monoids2.

(** The general associativity theorem. *)


M: monoid
l, s: list M
iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate l s) =
(iterop_list_mon l + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid


M: monoid
l, s: list M
iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate l s) =
(iterop_list_mon l + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid

  
M: monoid
s: list M
∏ l : list M,
iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate l s) =
(iterop_list_mon l + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
 
M: monoid
s: list M
iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate [] s) =
(iterop_list_mon [] + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
M: monoid
s: list M
∏ (x : M) (xs : list M),
iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate xs s) =
(iterop_list_mon xs + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
→ iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate (x :: xs) s) =
  (iterop_list_mon (x :: xs) + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid

  
M: monoid
s: list M
iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate [] s) =
(iterop_list_mon [] + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
 apply pathsinv0, lunax.
  
M: monoid
s: list M
∏ (x : M) (xs : list M),
iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate xs s) =
(iterop_list_mon xs + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
→ iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate (x :: xs) s) =
  (iterop_list_mon (x :: xs) + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
 
M: monoid
s: list M
x: M
xs: list M
J: iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate xs s) =
(iterop_list_mon xs + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate (x :: xs) s) =
(iterop_list_mon (x :: xs) + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
 
M: monoid
s: list M
x: M
xs: list M
J: iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate xs s) =
(iterop_list_mon xs + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
iterop_list_mon (x :: Lists.concatenate xs s) =
(iterop_list_mon (x :: xs) + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid

    
M: monoid
s: list M
x: M
xs: list M
J: iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate xs s) =
(iterop_list_mon xs + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op
  (x :: Lists.concatenate xs s) =
(iterop_list 0 op (x :: xs) + iterop_list 0 op s)%addmonoid

    
M: monoid
s: list M
x: M
xs: list M
J: iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate xs s) =
(iterop_list_mon xs + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
(x + iterop_list 0 op (Lists.concatenate xs s))%addmonoid =
(x + iterop_list 0 op xs + iterop_list 0 op s)%addmonoid

    
M: monoid
s: list M
x: M
xs: list M
J: iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate xs s) =
(iterop_list_mon xs + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
(x + iterop_list 0 op (Lists.concatenate xs s))%addmonoid =
(x + (iterop_list 0 op xs + iterop_list 0 op s))%addmonoid
 
M: monoid
s: list M
x: M
xs: list M
J: iterop_list_mon (Lists.concatenate xs s) =
(iterop_list_mon xs + iterop_list_mon s)%addmonoid
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.concatenate xs s) =
(iterop_list 0 op xs + iterop_list 0 op s)%addmonoid
 exact J.
Defined.


M: monoid
isAssociative_list 0%addmonoid op


M: monoid
isAssociative_list 0%addmonoid op

  (** This proof comes from the Associativity theorem, % \cite[section 1.3, Theorem 1, page 4]{BourbakiAlgebraI}. \par % *)
  (* this proof comes from the Associativity theorem, Bourbaki, Algebra, § 1.3, Theorem 1, page 4. *)
  
M: monoid
∏ x : list (list M),
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten x) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op x

  
M: monoid
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten []) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op []
M: monoid
∏ (x : list M) (xs : list (list M)),
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op xs
→ iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten (x :: xs)) =
  iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op (x :: xs)

  
M: monoid
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten []) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op []
 
M: monoid
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten []) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op []
 reflexivity.
  
M: monoid
∏ (x : list M) (xs : list (list M)),
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op xs
→ iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten (x :: xs)) =
  iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op (x :: xs)
 
M: monoid
x: list M
xs: list (list M)
I: iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op xs
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten (x :: xs)) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op (x :: xs)
 
M: monoid
x: list M
xs: list (list M)
I: iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op xs
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten (x :: xs)) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op (x :: xs)

    
M: monoid
x: list M
xs: list (list M)
I: iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op xs
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op
  (Lists.concatenate x (Lists.flatten xs)) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op (x :: xs)
 
M: monoid
x: list M
xs: list (list M)
I: iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op xs
(iterop_list_mon x +
 iterop_list_mon (Lists.flatten xs))%addmonoid =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op (x :: xs)

    
M: monoid
x: list M
xs: list (list M)
I: iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op xs
(iterop_list_mon x +
 iterop_list_mon (Lists.flatten xs))%addmonoid =
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op
  (map (iterop_list 0%addmonoid op) (x :: xs))
 
M: monoid
x: list M
xs: list (list M)
I: iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op xs
(iterop_list_mon x +
 iterop_list_mon (Lists.flatten xs))%addmonoid =
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op
  (iterop_list 0%addmonoid op x
   :: map (iterop_list 0%addmonoid op) xs)

    
M: monoid
x: list M
xs: list (list M)
I: iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op xs
(iterop_list_mon x +
 iterop_list_mon (Lists.flatten xs))%addmonoid =
(iterop_list 0 op x +
 iterop_list 0 op (map (iterop_list 0 op) xs))%addmonoid

    
M: monoid
x: list M
xs: list (list M)
I: iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op xs
(iterop_list_mon x +
 iterop_list_mon (Lists.flatten xs))%addmonoid =
(iterop_list 0 op x +
 iterop_list 0 op (map (iterop_list 0 op) xs))%addmonoid
 
M: monoid
x: list M
xs: list (list M)
I: iterop_list 0%addmonoid op (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list_list 0%addmonoid op xs
iterop_list_mon (Lists.flatten xs) =
iterop_list 0%addmonoid op
  (map (iterop_list 0%addmonoid op) xs)
 exact I.
Defined.

(** generalized commutativity *)

Local Notation "s □ x" := (append s x) (at level 64, left associativity).

Ltac change_lhs a := match goal with |- @paths ?T ?x ?y
                                     => change (@paths T x y) with (@paths T a y) end.
Ltac change_rhs a := match goal with |- @paths ?T ?x ?y
                                     => change (@paths T x y) with (@paths T x a) end.

⟦ stnsum f ⟧ ≃ ⟦ S n ⟧: ⟦ stnsum f ⟧ ≃ ⟦ S n ⟧
x':= x ∘ r: ∏ x : ⟦ stnsum f ⟧, (λ _ : ⟦ S n ⟧, M) (r x)
s0:= dni lastelement (dni lastelement lastelement): ⟦ 3 ⟧
s1:= dni lastelement lastelement: ⟦ 3 ⟧
s2:= lastelement: ⟦ 3 ⟧
f':= nil □ j □ n - j : ⟦ 2 ⟧ → nat: ⟦ 2 ⟧ → nat
B': n = n
r':= weqfibtototal (λ k : nat, k < n)
  (λ k : nat, k < n)
  (λ k : nat,
   eqweqmap (maponpaths (λ n : nat, k < n) B')): ⟦ n ⟧ ≃ ⟦ n ⟧
x'':= x ∘ dni (j,, jlt) ∘ r': ⟦ n ⟧ → M
i: ⟦ n ⟧
dni (j,, jlt)
  (totalfun (λ k : nat, natgtb n k = true)
     (λ k : nat, natgtb n k = true)
     (λ x : nat,
      eqweqmap
        (maponpaths (λ n : nat, natgtb n x = true) B'))
     i) = dni (j,, jlt) i

    reflexivity. }
Qed.

        (invmap (weqdnicompl i')
           (weqoncompl_ne f i (stnneq i) (stnneq i')
              (weqdnicompl lastelement (j,, J)))))

Definition MultipleOperation (X:UU) : UU := UnorderedSequence X → X.

Section Mult.

  Context {X:UU} (op : MultipleOperation X).

  
X: UU
op: MultipleOperation X
UnorderedSequence (UnorderedSequence X) → X

UnorderedSequence (UnorderedSequence X) → X

s: UnorderedSequence (UnorderedSequence X)
X
 exact (op (composeUnorderedSequence op s)).
  Defined.

  Definition isAssociativeMultipleOperation := ∏ x, op (flattenUnorderedSequence x) = composeMultipleOperation x.

End Mult.

Definition AssociativeMultipleOperation {X} := ∑ op:MultipleOperation X, isAssociativeMultipleOperation op.
